<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 1in"><b>Item&#160;5.07</b></td><td><b>Submission of Matters to a Vote of Security Holders. </b></td></tr></table>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><b>&#160;</b></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">At Tesla, Inc.&#8217;s (&#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Tesla</span>&#8221;) 2024 Annual Meeting
of Stockholders (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Annual Meeting</span>&#8221;) held on June 13, 2024, Tesla&#8217;s stockholders voted on the following twelve
proposals and Tesla&#8217;s inspector of election certified the vote tabulations indicated below<span style="background-color: white">.</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><b><span style="text-decoration: underline">Proposal 1</span></b></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">The individuals listed below were elected as Class
II directors at the Annual Meeting to serve on Tesla&#8217;s Board of Directors (&#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Board</span>&#8221;) for a term of three years
or until their respective successors are duly elected and qualified.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><b><span style="text-decoration: underline">Proposal 2</span></b></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 2pt 0pt 0; text-indent: 81pt">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Proposal 2 was a management proposal to approve
executive compensation on a non-binding advisory basis. This proposal was approved.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><b><span style="text-decoration: underline">Proposal 3</span></b></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 2pt 0pt 0; text-align: center">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Proposal 3 was a management proposal to approve
the redomestication of Tesla from Delaware to Texas by conversion. This proposal was approved. Approval of the proposal required the affirmative
vote of each of:</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>

  <td style="text-align: justify">the majority of outstanding shares of Tesla common stock entitled to vote on the proposal (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Conversion Standard</span>&#8221;),</td></tr>
</table>


<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>

in person or by proxy at the Annual Meeting and entitled to vote on the proposal (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Conversion Disinterested Standard</span>&#8221;).</td></tr>
</table>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><b><span style="text-decoration: underline">Proposal 4</span></b></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 2pt 0pt 0; text-align: center">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Proposal 4 was a management proposal to ratify
the 100% performance-based stock option award to Elon Musk that was proposed to and approved by our stockholders in 2018. This proposal

Standard</span>&#8221;),</td>
</tr></table>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Accordingly, the votes cast in factor of approving Proposal 4 constituted
approximately 72% of all votes cast in person or by proxy at the Annual Meeting on the proposal, excluding votes of shares owned, directly
or indirectly, by Messrs. Elon and Kimbal Musk.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><b>&#160;</b></p>

the appointment of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP as the Company&#8217;s independent registered public accounting firm for the fiscal year
ending December 31, 2024. This proposal was approved.</p>
